class="hidden lg:block text-sublabel text-accent !m-0 !my-0 !p-0">Transaction</span><div class="prose flex-1"><div class="flex flex-col gap-24 text-sm"><div class="flex flex-col gap-x-12 gap-y-4 method="POST" route="/partnerships/{partnershipId}/transaction-groups/{transactionGroupId}/generate-edi"><h1 class="text-[1.75em] font-semibold">Deliver Transaction Group</h1><p class="mb-8 text-lg text-primary">This endpoint generates and delivers a fully-formed EDI file containing the staged transactions in the specified transaction group.</p><div class="flex flex-row items-center gap-2.5 p-3 rounded-xl border bg-fd-card text-fd-card-foreground not-prose"><span class="method-nav-pill inline-flex items-center min-w-8"><span class="px-1 py-0.5 rounded-md text-[0.75rem] leading-tight xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon absolute transition-transform"><path d="M6.9998 6V3C6.9998 2.44772 7.44752 2 7.9998 2H19.9998C20.5521 2 text-secondary"><div class="flex divide-x divide-gray-200 overflow-x-auto px-2 [&amp;&gt;div:first-child]:pr-2 [&amp;&gt;div:last-child:not(:first-child)]:pl-2 [&amp;&gt;div:not(:first-child):not(:last-child)]:px-2"><div><a class="operation-target inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 p-1.5 no-underline hover:text-tertiary" href="https://github.com/Stedi/openApi/blob/main/core.json#:~:text=&quot;operationId&quot;%3A%20&quot;GenerateTransactionGroupEdi&quot;" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon text-tertiary"><path d="M4 18V14.3C4 13.4716 3.32843 12.8 2.5 12.8H2V11.2H2.5C3.32843 11.2 4 10.5284 4 9.7V6C4 4.34315 5.34315 3 7 3H8V5H7C6.44772 5 6 5.44772 6 6V10.1C6 10.9858 5.42408 11.7372 4.62623 12C5.42408 12.2628 6 13.0142 6 13.9V18C6 18.5523 6.44772 19 7 19H8V21H7C5.34315 21 4 19.6569 4 18ZM20 14.3V18C20 19.6569 18.6569 21 17 21H16V19H17C17.5523 19 18 18.5523 18 18V13.9C18 13.0142 18.5759 12.2628 19.3738 12C18.5759 11.7372 18 10.9858 18 10.1V6C18 5.44772 17.5523 5 17 5H16V3H17C18.6569 3 20 4.34315 20 6V9.7C20 10.5284 20.6716 11.2 21.5 11.2H22V12.8H21.5C20.6716 12.8 20 13.4716 20 14.3Z"></path></svg>OpenAPI spec</a></div></div></div><p>When you call this endpoint, Stedi:</p>
<ol>
<li>Generates a single EDI file containing all transactions in the specified transaction group (<code>transactionGroupId</code>). This includes adding required envelope information (<code>ISA</code> and <code>GS</code> headers) and autogenerated control numbers.</li>
<li>Delivers the EDI file to your trading partner through the connection specified in the transaction settings.</li>
</ol>
<span class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-lg flex gap-3 border border-amber-100 bg-amber-50 dark:border-amber-950 dark:bg-amber-500/10" data-callout-type="warning"><span class="flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-6 flex items-center justify-center text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-300" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon "><path d="M12 22C6.47715 22 2 17.5228 2 12C2 6.47715 6.47715 2 12 2C17.5228 2 22 6.47715 22 12C22 17.5228 17.5228 22 12 22ZM11 15V17H13V15H11ZM11 7V13H13V7H11Z"></path></svg></span><span class="prose min-w-0 w-full text-amber-900 dark:text-amber-200" data-component-part="callout-content"><p>You can only call this endpoint with a given <code>transactionGroupId</code> once.
Afterward, that transaction group is locked, and you must create a new
transaction group to generate another file.</p></span></span>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="stage-transactions"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#stage-transactions"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Stage transactions</a></h2>
<p>You can use the <a href="/docs/edi-platform/api-reference/core/stage-transactions">Stage Transactions API</a> to store one or more transactions in a transaction group on Stedi. When you&#x27;re ready to send all of the transactions in the group, you can call this endpoint to generate and deliver an EDI file to your trading partner.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="delivery-attempts"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#delivery-attempts"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Delivery attempts</a></h2>
<p>Stedi attempts to deliver a file to all configured connections every 6 minutes for up to 3 total attempts. If it cannot deliver the file after the third attempt, it marks the file execution as <code>FAILED</code> and emits the <a href="/docs/edi-platform/operate/event-types#file-failed"><code>file.failed.v2</code> event</a>. Stedi displays each delivery attempt and the failure details on the <a href="https://portal.stedi.com/app/core/file-executions" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Files</a> page.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="customize-generated-files"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#customize-generated-files"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Customize generated files</a></h2>
<p>You can change the timezone, time format, character set (which characters are allowed), and filename for generated files. <a href="/docs/edi-platform/operate/generate-edi#timezone-and-time-format">Learn more</a>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="inbound-processing"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#inbound-processing"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Inbound processing</a></h2>
<p>There is no equivalent endpoint for parsing EDI files into JSON. To parse inbound files, you or your partner can send EDI files to an SFTP/FTPS or AS2 <a href="/docs/edi-platform/configure/trading-partners/connections">connection</a>, and Stedi sends the JSON payload to the configured <a href="/docs/edi-platform/configure/destinations">Destination webhook</a>.</p>
<p>This endpoint generates and delivers a fully-formed EDI file for a given transaction group. Transactions are staged in a group using the <code>CreateTransactionGroup</code> endpoint. Once a file has been generated for a given transaction group, the group can no longer be used.</p><div class="flex items-end justify-between gap-2"><h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center
